caterwaul

.

./Adjunction

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : dObject → cObject)
→ ∀(g : cObject → dObject)
→ Type
type
  λ(cObject : Kind)
→ λ(dObject : Kind)
→ λ(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ λ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ(f : dObject → cObject)
→ λ(g : cObject → dObject)
→ { counit :
      ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = f (g a), _2 = a }
  , leftAdjunct :
        ∀(a : dObject)
      → ∀(b : cObject)
      → v.arrow
        { _1 = c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = b }, _2 = d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b } }
  , rightAdjunct :
        ∀(a : dObject)
      → ∀(b : cObject)
      → v.arrow
        { _1 = d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b }, _2 = c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = b } }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g (f a) }
  }

impliedComonad (term)

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : dObject → cObject)
→ ∀ ( functor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : dObject)
          → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
      }
    )
→ ∀(g : cObject → dObject)
→ ∀ ( adjunction
    : { counit :
          ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = f (g a), _2 = a }
      , leftAdjunct :
            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = b }
          → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b }
      , rightAdjunct :
            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b }
          → c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = b }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g (f a) }
      }
    )
→ { product :
      ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = f (g a), _2 = f (g (f (g a))) }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = f (g a), _2 = a }
  }

impliedMonad (term)

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : dObject → cObject)
→ ∀(g : cObject → dObject)
→ ∀ ( functor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : cObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → d.arrow { _1 = g a, _2 = g b }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( adjunction
    : { counit :
          ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = f (g a), _2 = a }
      , leftAdjunct :
            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = b }
          → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b }
      , rightAdjunct :
            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b }
          → c.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = b }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g (f a) }
      }
    )
→ { product :
      ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = g (f (g (f a))), _2 = g (f a) }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g (f a) }
  }

./Arrow

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ { fanout :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = c }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
  , lmap :
        ∀(h : object)
      → ∀(i : object)
      → ∀(j : object)
      → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = h }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
  , map :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            v.product
            { _1 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = b._1, _2 = a._1 }
            , _2 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
        , _2 =
            v.arrow { _1 = cat.arrow a, _2 = cat.arrow b }
        }
  , product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , rmap :
        ∀(h : object)
      → ∀(i : object)
      → ∀(j : object)
      → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = i }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
  , split :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → ∀(d : object)
      → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
      → cat.arrow { _1 = c, _2 = d }
      → cat.arrow
        { _1 =
            cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
        , _2 =
            cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = d }
        }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

extractCategory (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( arrow
    : { fanout :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = c }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
      , lmap :
            ∀(h : object)
          → ∀(i : object)
          → ∀(j : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = h }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = b._1, _2 = a._1 }
                , _2 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                v.arrow { _1 = cat.arrow a, _2 = cat.arrow b }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rmap :
            ∀(h : object)
          → ∀(i : object)
          → ∀(j : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = i }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
      , split :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → ∀(d : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = c, _2 = d }
          → cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
            , _2 =
                cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = d }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v

          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( arrow
    : { fanout :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = c }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
      , lmap :

          → ∀(i : object)
          → ∀(j : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = h }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = b._1, _2 = a._1 }
                , _2 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                v.arrow { _1 = cat.arrow a, _2 = cat.arrow b }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rmap :
            ∀(h : object)
          → ∀(i : object)
          → ∀(j : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = i }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }

          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)

          → cat.arrow

                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
            , _2 =
                cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = d }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { map :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })

      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            v.product
            { _1 =

                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }

  }

extractSemigroupoid (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( arrow
    : { fanout :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = c }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
      , lmap :
            ∀(h : object)
          → ∀(i : object)
          → ∀(j : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = h }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = b._1, _2 = a._1 }
                , _2 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                v.arrow { _1 = cat.arrow a, _2 = cat.arrow b }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rmap :
            ∀(h : object)
          → ∀(i : object)
          → ∀(j : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = i, _2 = j }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = i }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = h, _2 = j }
      , split :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → ∀(d : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = c, _2 = d }
          → cat.arrow

                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }

            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )

          → (   ∀(z : object)

              → r

./Bimonad

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object → object)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object → object)
→ { comonoid :
      { product :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = m a, _2 = m (m a) }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = m a, _2 = a }
      }
  , monoid :
      { product :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = m (m a), _2 = m a }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = m a }
      }
  }

./Bimonoid

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object)
→ { comonoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m } }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.unit }
      }
  , monoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

./Bool

eq (term)

type
{ eq : ∀(x : Bool) → ∀(y : Bool) → Bool }

lattice (term)

type
{ join :

, meet :

}

./Category/Cartesian

Kind (kind)

{- Can’t define `augmentation` at this level, because we have no unit `Kind`. -}

sort
  ∀(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(object : Kind)
→ Kind
kind
  λ(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ λ(vObject : Kind)
→ λ(object : Kind)
→ { arrow :
      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) vObject
  , constraint :
      object → Type
  , diagonal :
      cat.arrow object (cat.product object object)
  , product :
      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object
  , unit :
      object
  }

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object)
→ { category :
      { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
  , comonoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m } }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.unit }
      }
  , monoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

impliedBimonoid (term)

{- Every monoid in a cartesian category is a bimonoid in a unique way. -}

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ ∀ ( cartesian
    : { category :
          { product :
                ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
              → (   ∀(r : Type)
                  → (   ∀(z : object)
                      → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                      → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                      → r
                    )
                  → r
                )
              → cat.arrow a
          , unit :
              ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
          }
      , comonoid :
          { product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m } }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.unit }
          }
      , monoid :
          { product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( monoid
    : { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
    )
→ { comonoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m } }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.unit }
      }
  , monoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

impliedHopfMonoid (term)

{- Every group in a cartesian category is a Hopf monoid in a unique way. -}

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ ∀ ( cartesian
    : { category :
          { product :
                ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
              → (   ∀(r : Type)
                  → (   ∀(z : object)
                      → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                      → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                      → r
                    )
                  → r
                )
              → cat.arrow a
          , unit :
              ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
          }
      , comonoid :
          { product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m } }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.unit }
          }
      , monoid :
          { product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( group
    : { inverse :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
      , product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
    )
→ { antipode :
      cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
  , comonoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m } }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = cat.unit }
      }
  , monoid :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

./Category/Dagger

Kind (term)

{- A true †-category has a contravariant endofunctor on C that reverses the morphisms. I’m not sure how to implement that, so this structure simply uses pairs of morphisms as the morphism. -}

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ { arrow :
      ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → Type
  , constraint :
      object → Type
  }

category (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → ∀ ( p
          :   ∀(r : Type)
            → (   ∀(z : object)
                → { from :
                      cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = z }
                  , to :
                      cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  }
                → { from :
                      cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._1 }
                  , to :
                      cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  }
                → r
              )
            → r
          )
      → { from : cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = a._1 }, to : cat.arrow a }
  , unit :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
        , to :
            cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
        }
  }

Type (type)

{- TODO: Ideally, the diamond and star monoids shouldn’t _also_ have the category members (as they just duplicate the ones on the rig), but it was more trouble to avoid them for the time being. -}

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , diamond :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      , star :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      }
    )
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , diamond :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      , star :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      }
    )
→ { combine :
      cat.arrow
      { _1 =
          ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
          ).product
          { _1 =
              ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
              ).unit
          , _2 =
              ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
              ).unit
          }
      , _2 =
          (cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }).unit
      }
  , diamond :
      { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = b, _2 = c }
                    }
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        c
                    }
                }
            , to :
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        c
                    }
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = b, _2 = c }
                    }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    , _2 =
                        a
                    }
                }
            , to :
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    , _2 =
                        a
                    }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    a
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    b
                }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
            ).arrow
            a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    }
                }
            , to :
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.diamond
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.diamond
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , unit :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
            ).arrow
            { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
  , product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , split :
      cat.arrow
      { _1 =
          ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
          ).unit
      , _2 =
          ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
          ).product
          { _1 =
              ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
              ).unit
          , _2 =
              ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
              ).unit
          }
      }
  , star :
      { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = b, _2 = c }
                    }
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        c
                    }
                }
            , to :
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        c
                    }
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).product
                        { _1 = b, _2 = c }
                    }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    , _2 =
                        a
                    }
                }
            , to :
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    , _2 =
                        a
                    }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    a
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    b
                }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).arrow
                    { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
            ).arrow
            a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    }
                }
            , to :
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).arrow
                { _1 =
                    (   cat.star
                      ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                    ).product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        (   cat.star
                          ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                        ).unit
                    }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , unit :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
            ).arrow
            { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
  , swap :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → ∀(d : object)
      → cat.arrow
        { _1 =
            ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
            ).product
            { _1 =
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).product
                { _1 = a, _2 = b }
            , _2 =
                ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).product
                { _1 = c, _2 = d }
            }
        , _2 =
            ( cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
            ).product
            { _1 =
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).product
                { _1 = a, _2 = c }
            , _2 =
                (   cat.diamond
                  ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
                ).product
                { _1 = b, _2 = d }
            }
        }
  , switch :
      cat.arrow
      { _1 =
          ( cat.diamond ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }
          ).unit
      , _2 =
          (cat.star ∧ { arrow = cat.arrow, constraint = cat.constraint }).unit
      }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

./Category/Endofunctor

duoidal (term)

{- NB: This is defined in terms of the monoidal categories instead of the other way around because this is more restrictive than either monoidal category. • Applicative requires that the target category is **Set** and • monadic requires an endofunctor`object`. When you combine these two restrictions, you end up only being able to support endofunctors in **Set**. -}

type
  ∀(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ { arrow :
      ∀(f : { _1 : Type → Type, _2 : Type → Type }) → Type
  , constraint :
      ∀(f : Type → Type) → Type
  , diamond :
      { product :
          ∀(f : { _1 : Type → Type, _2 : Type → Type }) → ∀(a : Type) → Type
      , unit :
          ∀(x : Type) → Type
      }
  , star :
      { product :
          ∀(f : { _1 : Type → Type, _2 : Type → Type }) → ∀(a : Type) → Type
      , unit :
          ∀(a : Type) → Type
      }
  }

      , product :

      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ { arrow :

  , constraint :
      ∀(f : Type → Type) → Type
  , product :
      ∀(f : { _1 : Type → Type, _2 : Type → Type }) → ∀(a : Type) → Type

      ∀(x : Type) → Type
  }

category (term)

{- This cheats a bit on the unit, since `dObject` is Type, we don’t need a functor **Set** → 𝒟. -}

  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )

      ∀(f : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject }) → Type
  , constraint :
      ∀(f : cObject → dObject) → Type
  }

inducedFunctor (term)

{- Any functor `p : C → C'` induces a functor between functor categories `[C', D] → [C, D]`. -}

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(cpObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cp
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cpObject, _2 : cpObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cpObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(p : cObject → cpObject)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ { map :
        ∀(a : cpObject → dObject)
      → ∀(b : cpObject → dObject)
      → ∀(fn : ∀(a : cpObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a@1 a, _2 = b a })
      → ∀(i : cObject)
      → d.arrow { _1 = a (p i), _2 = b (p i) }
  }

types.dhall (term)

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ { Adjunction :
        ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → ∀(g : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → Type
  , Bifunctor :
        ∀ ( f
          :   { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject }
            → cObject
            → dObject
          )
      → Type
  , Category :
        ∀ ( v
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            , product :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , unit :
                Type
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( cat
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject } → Type
            , constraint :
                (cObject → dObject) → Type
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Codensity :
        ∀ ( d
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(m : (cObject → dObject) → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Comonad :
      ∀(m : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject) → Type
  , Compose :
        ∀ ( f
          : { _1 :
                (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject
            , _2 :
                (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject
            }
          )
      → ∀(a : cObject → dObject)
      → cObject
      → dObject
  , Const :
        ∀(a : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject })
      → cObject
      → dObject
  , Costar :
        ∀(m : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → ∀(a : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject })
      → Type
  , Coyoneda :
      ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → Type) → ∀(a : cObject → dObject) → Type
  , Density :
        ∀ ( d
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Endofunctor :
      ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject) → Type
  , HomFunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject } → Type) → Type
  , Identity :
      ∀(a : cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject
  , Lan :
        ∀(p : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → Type)
      → ∀(a : cObject → dObject)
      → Type
  , Leibniz :
      { arrow :
          ∀(a : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject }) → Type
      , constraint :
          ∀(f : cObject → dObject) → Type
      }
  , Monad :
      ∀(m : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject) → Type
  , NaturalTransformation :
        ∀ ( f
          : { _1 :
                (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject
            , _2 :
                (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Profunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject } → Type) → Type
  , Ran :
        ∀(p : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → Type)
      → ∀(a : cObject → dObject)
      → Type
  , Semigroupoid :
        ∀ ( v
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            , product :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , unit :
                Type
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( cat
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject } → Type
            , constraint :
                (cObject → dObject) → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(m : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject } → Type)
      → Type
  , Star :
        ∀(m : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → ∀(a : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject })
      → Type
  , Strong :
      ∀(f : { _1 : cObject → dObject, _2 : cObject → dObject } → Type) → Type
  , Traversable :
        ∀(m : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → cObject → dObject)
      → Type
  , Yoneda :
      ∀(f : (cObject → dObject) → Type) → ∀(a : cObject → dObject) → Type
  }

./Category/Monoidal

./Category/Monoidal/Braided

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ { associativity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            , _2 =
                cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
            , _2 =
                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            }
        }
  , braid :
        ∀(x : object)
      → ∀(y : object)
      → cat.arrow
        { _1 =
            cat.product { _1 = x, _2 = y }
        , _2 =
            cat.product { _1 = y, _2 = x }
        }
  , leftIdentity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a } }
        , to :
            cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
        }
  , map :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            v.product
            { _1 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
        , _2 =
            cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
        }
  , product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , rightIdentity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit } }
        , to :
            cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit }, _2 = a }
        }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

./Category/Monoidal/Cartesian

Kind (kind)

{- Can’t define `augmentation` at this level, because we have no unit `Kind`. -}

sort
  ∀(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(object : Kind)
→ Kind
kind
  λ(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ λ(vObject : Kind)
→ λ(object : Kind)
→ { arrow :
      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) vObject
  , constraint :
      object → Type
  , diagonal :
      cat.arrow object (cat.product object object)
  , product :
      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object
  , unit :
      object

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ { associativity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            , _2 =
                cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
            , _2 =
                cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            }
        }
  , braid :
        ∀(x : object)
      → ∀(y : object)
      → cat.arrow
        { _1 =
            cat.product { _1 = x, _2 = y }
        , _2 =
            cat.product { _1 = y, _2 = x }
        }
  , leftIdentity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a } }
        , to :
            cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
        }
  , map :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            v.product
            { _1 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
        , _2 =
            cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
        }
  , product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , rightIdentity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit } }
        , to :
            cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit }, _2 = a }
        }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

category (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → ∀ ( p
          :   ∀(r : Type)
            → (   ∀(z : object)
                → cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = z }
                → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._1 }
                → r
              )
            → r
          )
      → cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = a._1 }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

categorySort (term)

type
  ∀(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ { arrow : ∀(a : Kind) → ∀(b : Kind) → Kind }

      , diamond :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      , star :

  , constraint :
      object → Type
  , diamond :
      { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
  , star :

  }

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ { Adjunction :
      ∀(f : object → object) → ∀(g : object → object) → Type
  , Arrow :
      Type
  , Bifunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object) → Type
  , Category :
        ∀ ( v
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :

                Type
            }

                object → Type
            }

      → Type
  , Codensity :

                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(m : object → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , CommutativeGroup :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , CommutativeMonoid :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , Comonad :
      ∀(m : object → object) → Type
  , Compose :
        ∀(f : { _1 : object → object, _2 : object → object })
      → ∀(a : object)
      → object
  , Const :
      ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → object
  , Costar :
      ∀(m : object → object) → ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → Type
  , Coyoneda :
      ∀(f : object → Type) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  , Day :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object → Type, _2 : object → Type }) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  , Density :
        ∀ ( d
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(f : object → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Endofunctor :
      ∀(f : object → object) → Type
  , Field :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , Group :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , HomFunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
  , Identity :
      ∀(a : object) → object
  , Lan :
      ∀(p : object → object) → ∀(f : object → Type) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  , Leibniz :
      { arrow :
          ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → Type

          object → Type
      }
  , Monad :

  , Monoid :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , MonoidalFunctor :
      ∀(f : object → Type) → Type
  , NaturalTransformation :

  , Profunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
  , Ran :

  , Rig :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , Ring :

  , Semigroup :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , Semigroupoid :

                Type
            }

Kind (term)

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ { arrow :
        ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            , _2 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            }
          )
      → Type
  , constraint :
      ∀(x : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }) → Type
  }

Type (term)

type
  ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → vObject
      , unit :
          vObject
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ { arrow :
        ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            , _2 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            }
          )

  , constraint :
      ∀(obj : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }) → Type

category (term)

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cCategory
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : cObject)
                  → c.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → c.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → c.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( dCategory
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : dObject)
                  → d.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → d.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → d.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { product :
        ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            , _2 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( p
          :   ∀(r : Type)
            → (   ∀(z : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
                → { _1 :
                      c.arrow { _1 = z._1, _2 = a._2._1 }
                  , _2 :
                      d.arrow { _1 = z._2, _2 = a._2._2 }
                  }
                → { _1 :
                      c.arrow { _1 = a._1._1, _2 = z._1 }
                  , _2 :
                      d.arrow { _1 = a._1._2, _2 = z._2 }
                  }
                → r
              )
            → r
          )
      → { _1 :
            c.arrow { _1 = a._1._1, _2 = a._2._1 }
        , _2 :
            d.arrow { _1 = a._1._2, _2 = a._2._2 }
        }
  , unit :
        ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
      → { _1 :
            c.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = a._1 }
        , _2 :
            d.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = a._2 }
        }
  }

                Type
            }

                  }
                → Type
            , constraint :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Codensity :

          : { arrow :

            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(m : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Comonad :
        ∀(m : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
      → Type
  , Compose :
        ∀ ( f
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            , _2 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            }
          )
      → ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })

  , Const :
        ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            , _2 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            }
          )
      → { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
  , Costar :
        ∀(m : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })

            , _2 :
                { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject }
            }
          )

        ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            , _2 :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            }
          )
      → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
      → Type
  , Costar :
        ∀ ( m
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
            → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
            → Type
          )
      → ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            , _2 :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Coyoneda :
        ∀(f : ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type)
      → ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
      → Type
  , Density :
        ∀ ( d
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(f : ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Endofunctor :
        ∀ ( f
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
            → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
            → Type
          )
      → Type
  , HomFunctor :
        ∀ ( f
          :   { _1 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              , _2 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              }
            → Type
          )
      → Type
  , Identity :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
      → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
      → Type
  , Lan :
        ∀ ( p
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
            → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
            → Type
          )
      → ∀(f : ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type)
      → ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
      → Type
  , Leibniz :
      { arrow :
            ∀ ( a
              : { _1 :
                    { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
                , _2 :
                    { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
                }
              )
          → Type
      , constraint :
          ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
      }
  , Monad :
        ∀ ( m
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
            → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
            → Type
          )
      → Type
  , NaturalTransformation :
        ∀ ( f
          : { _1 :
                  ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
                → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
                → Type
            , _2 :
                  ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
                → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
                → Type
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Profunctor :
        ∀ ( f
          :   { _1 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              , _2 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              }
            → Type
          )
      → Type
  , Ran :
        ∀ ( p
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
            → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
            → Type
          )
      → ∀(f : ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type)
      → ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
      → Type
  , Semigroup :
      ∀(m : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
  , Semigroupoid :
        ∀ ( v
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            , product :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , unit :
                Type
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( cat
          : { arrow :
                  { _1 :
                      { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
                  , _2 :
                      { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
                  }
                → Type
            , constraint :
                ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( m
          :   { _1 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              , _2 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              }
            → Type
          )
      → Type
  , Star :
        ∀ ( m
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
            → { _1 : object, _2 : object }
            → Type
          )
      → ∀ ( a
          : { _1 :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            , _2 :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Strong :
        ∀ ( f
          :   { _1 :

              , _2 :
                  { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
              }
            → Type
          )
      → Type

        ∀ ( m
          :   ({ _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)

./Category/Rig

Kind (kind)

sort
  ∀(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(object : Kind)
→ Kind
kind
  λ(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ λ(vObject : Kind)
→ λ(object : Kind)
→ { additive :
      { product : cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object, unit : object }
  , arrow :
      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) vObject
  , constraint :
      object → Type
  , multiplicative :
      { product : cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object, unit : object }
  }

Type (type)

{- TODO: Ideally, the additive and multiplicative monoids shouldn’t _also_ have the category members (as they just duplicate the ones on the rig), but it was more trouble to avoid them for the time being. -}

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { additive :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      , arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , multiplicative :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      }
    )
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { additive :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      , arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , multiplicative :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      }
    )
→ { additive :
      { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.additive.product
                    { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                , _2 =
                    cat.additive.product
                    { _1 = cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.additive.product
                    { _1 = cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                , _2 =
                    cat.additive.product
                    { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    cat.additive.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.additive.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
                , _2 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                cat.arrow
                { _1 = cat.additive.product a, _2 = cat.additive.product b }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
  , distributivity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
                }
            , _2 =
                cat.multiplicative.product
                { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.multiplicative.product
                { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
                }
            }
        }
  , leftAnnihilation :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.unit
            , _2 =
                cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.unit
            }
        }
  , multiplicative :
      { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = b, _2 = c }
                    }
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        c
                    }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        c
                    }
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = b, _2 = c }
                    }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 = cat.multiplicative.unit, _2 = a }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 = cat.multiplicative.unit, _2 = a }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → v.arrow
            { _1 =
                v.product
                { _1 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
                , _2 =
                    cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                }
            , _2 =
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product a
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product b
                }
            }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    a
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 = a, _2 = cat.multiplicative.unit }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 = a, _2 = cat.multiplicative.unit }
                , _2 =
                    a
                }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
  , product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , rightAnnihilation :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.unit
            , _2 =
                cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.unit
            }
        }
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
