→ ∀ ( rig
    : { additive :
          { product :
              cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object
          , unit :
              object
          }
      , arrow :
          cat.arrow (cat.product object object) vObject
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , multiplicative :
          { product :
              cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object
          , unit :
              object
          }
      }
    )

      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) vObject
  , constraint :
      object → Type
  , product :
      cat.arrow (cat.product object object) object
  , unit :
      object

          }

            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })

            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { associativity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(c : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.product
                { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.product
                { _1 = cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.product
                { _1 = cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.product
                { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
            }
        }
  , leftIdentity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                a
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
            , _2 =
                a
            }
        }
  , map :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            v.product
            { _1 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 =
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
        , _2 =
            cat.arrow
            { _1 = cat.additive.product a, _2 = cat.additive.product b }
        }
  , product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , rightIdentity :
        ∀(a : object)
      → { from :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                a
            , _2 =
                cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
            }
        , to :
            cat.arrow
            { _1 =
                cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
            , _2 =
                a
            }
        }

  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :

      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { additive :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      , arrow :

      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , multiplicative :
          { product : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object, unit : object }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( rig
    : { additive :
          { associativity :
                ∀(a : object)
              → ∀(b : object)
              → ∀(c : object)
              → { from :
                    cat.arrow
                    { _1 =
                        cat.additive.product
                        { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                    , _2 =
                        cat.additive.product
                        { _1 = cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                    }
                , to :
                    cat.arrow
                    { _1 =
                        cat.additive.product
                        { _1 = cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                    , _2 =
                        cat.additive.product
                        { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                    }
                }
          , leftIdentity :
                ∀(a : object)
              → { from :
                    cat.arrow
                    { _1 =
                        a
                    , _2 =
                        cat.additive.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
                    }
                , to :
                    cat.arrow
                    { _1 =
                        cat.additive.product { _1 = cat.additive.unit, _2 = a }
                    , _2 =
                        a
                    }
                }
          , map :

              → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
              → v.arrow
                { _1 =
                    v.product
                    { _1 =
                        cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
                    , _2 =
                        cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
                    }
                , _2 =
                    cat.arrow
                    { _1 = cat.additive.product a, _2 = cat.additive.product b }
                }
          , product :
                ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
              → (   ∀(r : Type)
                  → (   ∀(z : object)
                      → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                      → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                      → r
                    )
                  → r
                )
              → cat.arrow a

                    cat.arrow
                    { _1 =
                        cat.additive.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.unit }
                    , _2 =
                        a
                    }
                }
          , unit :
              ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
          }
      , distributivity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.additive.product
                    { _1 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }
                    , _2 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
                    }
                , _2 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.multiplicative.product
                    { _1 = a, _2 = cat.additive.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }

                    cat.additive.product
                    { _1 =
                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }

                        cat.multiplicative.product { _1 = a, _2 = c }
                    }
                }
            }
      , leftAnnihilation :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.additive.unit
                , _2 =

types.dhall (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ { Adjunction :
      ∀(f : object → object) → ∀(g : object → object) → Type
  , Arrow :
      Type
  , Bifunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object) → Type
  , Category :
        ∀ ( v
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            , product :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , unit :
                Type
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( cat
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            , constraint :
                object → Type
            }
          )
      → Type
  , Codensity :
        ∀ ( d
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(m : object → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Comonad :
      ∀(m : object → object) → Type
  , Compose :
        ∀(f : { _1 : object → object, _2 : object → object })
      → ∀(a : object)
      → object
  , Const :
      ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → object
  , Costar :
      ∀(m : object → object) → ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → Type
  , Coyoneda :
      ∀(f : object → Type) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  , Density :
        ∀ ( d
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(f : object → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type
  , Endofunctor :
      ∀(f : object → object) → Type
  , HomFunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
  , Identity :
      ∀(a : object) → object
  , Lan :
      ∀(p : object → object) → ∀(f : object → Type) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  , Leibniz :
      { arrow :
          ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
  , Monad :
      ∀(m : object → object) → Type
  , NaturalTransformation :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object → object, _2 : object → object }) → Type
  , Profunctor :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
  , Ran :
      ∀(p : object → object) → ∀(f : object → Type) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  , Semigroup :
      ∀(m : object) → Type
  , Semigroupoid :
        ∀ ( v
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , constraint :
                Type → Type
            , product :
                { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
            , unit :
                Type
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( cat
          : { arrow :
                { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
            , constraint :
                object → Type
            }
          )
      → ∀(m : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
      → Type
  , Star :
      ∀(m : object → object) → ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object }) → Type
  , Strong :
      ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type) → Type
  , Traversable :
      ∀(m : object → object) → ∀(f : object → object) → Type
  , Yoneda :
      ∀(f : object → Type) → ∀(a : object) → Type
  }

arrow (term)

type
{ fanout :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → ∀(b : Type)
    → ∀(c : Type)
    → ∀(f : a → b)
    → ∀(g : a → c)
    → ∀(x : a)
    → { _1 : b, _2 : c }
, lmap :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → ∀(b : Type)
    → ∀(c : Type)
    → ∀(f : b → a)
    → ∀(p : a → c)
    → ∀(x : b)
    → c
, map :
      ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(b : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(f : { _1 : b._1 → a._1, _2 : a._2 → b._2 })
    → ∀(fn : a._1 → a._2)
    → ∀(x : b._1)
    → b._2
, product :
      ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(p : ∀(r : Type) → (∀(z : Type) → (z → a._2) → (a._1 → z) → r) → r)
    → a._1
    → a._2
, rmap :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → ∀(b : Type)
    → ∀(c : Type)
    → ∀(f : b → c)
    → ∀(p : a → b)
    → ∀(x : a)
    → c
, split :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → ∀(b : Type)
    → ∀(c : Type)
    → ∀(d : Type)
    → ∀(f : a → b)
    → ∀(g : c → d)
    → ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : c })
    → { _1 : b, _2 : d }
, unit :
    ∀(a : Type) → ∀(x : a) → a
}

    → ∀(p : ∀(r : Type) → (∀(z : Type) → (z → a._2) → (a._1 → z) → r) → r)
    → a._1
    → a._2
, unit :
    ∀(a : Type) → ∀(x : a) → a
}

monoidal (term)

type
{ associativity :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → ∀(b : Type)
    → ∀(c : Type)
    → { from :
            ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : { _1 : b, _2 : c } })
          → { _1 : { _1 : a, _2 : b }, _2 : c }
      , to :
            ∀(p : { _1 : { _1 : a, _2 : b }, _2 : c })
          → { _1 : a, _2 : { _1 : b, _2 : c } }
      }
, leftIdentity :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → { from :
          ∀(x : a) → { _1 : {}, _2 : a }
      , to :
          ∀(p : { _1 : {}, _2 : a }) → a
      }
, map :
      ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(b : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(f : { _1 : a._1 → b._1, _2 : a._2 → b._2 })
    → ∀(t : { _1 : a._1, _2 : a._2 })
    → { _1 : b._1, _2 : b._2 }
, product :
      ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(p : ∀(r : Type) → (∀(z : Type) → (z → a._2) → (a._1 → z) → r) → r)
    → a._1
    → a._2
, rightIdentity :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → { from :
          ∀(x : a) → { _1 : a, _2 : {} }
      , to :
          ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : {} }) → a
      }
, unit :
    ∀(a : Type) → ∀(x : a) → a
}

rig (term)

type
{ additive :
    { associativity :
          ∀(a : Type)
        → ∀(b : Type)
        → ∀(c : Type)
        → { from :
                ∀(e : < Left : a | Right : < Left : b | Right : c > >)
              → < Left : < Left : a | Right : b > | Right : c >
          , to :
                ∀(e : < Left : < Left : a | Right : b > | Right : c >)
              → < Left : a | Right : < Left : b | Right : c > >
          }
    , leftIdentity :
          ∀(a : Type)
        → { from :
              ∀(Right : a) → < Left : <> | Right : a >
          , to :
              ∀(e : < Left : <> | Right : a >) → a
          }
    , map :
          ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
        → ∀(b : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
        → ∀(f : { _1 : a._1 → b._1, _2 : a._2 → b._2 })
        → ∀(e : < Left : a._1 | Right : a._2 >)
        → < Left : b._1 | Right : b._2 >
    , product :
          ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
        → ∀(p : ∀(r : Type) → (∀(z : Type) → (z → a._2) → (a._1 → z) → r) → r)
        → a._1
        → a._2
    , rightIdentity :
          ∀(a : Type)
        → { from :
              ∀(Left : a) → < Left : a | Right : <> >
          , to :
              ∀(e : < Left : a | Right : <> >) → a
          }
    , unit :
        ∀(a : Type) → ∀(x : a) → a
    }
, distributivity :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → ∀(b : Type)
    → ∀(c : Type)
    → { from :
            ∀(e : < Left : { _1 : a, _2 : b } | Right : { _1 : a, _2 : c } >)
          → { _1 : a, _2 : < Left : b | Right : c > }
      , to :
            ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : < Left : b | Right : c > })
          → < Left : { _1 : a, _2 : b } | Right : { _1 : a, _2 : c } >
      }
, leftAnnihilation :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → { from :
          ∀(v : <>) → { _1 : <>, _2 : a }
      , to :
          ∀(p : { _1 : <>, _2 : a }) → <>
      }
, multiplicative :
    { associativity :
          ∀(a : Type)
        → ∀(b : Type)
        → ∀(c : Type)
        → { from :
                ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : { _1 : b, _2 : c } })
              → { _1 : { _1 : a, _2 : b }, _2 : c }
          , to :
                ∀(p : { _1 : { _1 : a, _2 : b }, _2 : c })
              → { _1 : a, _2 : { _1 : b, _2 : c } }
          }
    , leftIdentity :
          ∀(a : Type)
        → { from :
              ∀(x : a) → { _1 : {}, _2 : a }
          , to :
              ∀(p : { _1 : {}, _2 : a }) → a
          }
    , map :
          ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
        → ∀(b : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
        → ∀(f : { _1 : a._1 → b._1, _2 : a._2 → b._2 })
        → ∀(t : { _1 : a._1, _2 : a._2 })
        → { _1 : b._1, _2 : b._2 }
    , product :
          ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
        → ∀(p : ∀(r : Type) → (∀(z : Type) → (z → a._2) → (a._1 → z) → r) → r)
        → a._1
        → a._2
    , rightIdentity :
          ∀(a : Type)
        → { from :
              ∀(x : a) → { _1 : a, _2 : {} }
          , to :
              ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : {} }) → a
          }
    , unit :
        ∀(a : Type) → ∀(x : a) → a
    }
, product :
      ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
    → ∀(p : ∀(r : Type) → (∀(z : Type) → (z → a._2) → (a._1 → z) → r) → r)
    → a._1
    → a._2
, rightAnnihilation :
      ∀(a : Type)
    → { from :
          ∀(v : <>) → { _1 : a, _2 : <> }
      , to :
          ∀(p : { _1 : a, _2 : <> }) → <>
      }
, unit :
    ∀(a : Type) → ∀(x : a) → a
}

    )

      → ∀(m : Type → Type)
      → ∀(a : Type)
      → Type

            }

      → ∀(f : Type → Type)

Type (type)

{- FIXME: This should use `./../Monoid/Type … (./../Category/Monoidal/Profunctor object morphism)`, but the unit in that monoidal category definition isn’t correct (or, if it is, I can’t figure out how to use it). So instead, we just build the `Semigroup`, and then write a custom unit. But this means we’re not structurally a `Monoid`. -}

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ { product :
        ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
              → r
            )
          → r
        )
      → cat.arrow a
  , unit :
      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
  }

      }
    )

      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ { product :

      → (   ∀(r : Type)
          → (   ∀(z : object)
              → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
              → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }

postcomposition (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(c : object)
→ { map :
        ∀(x : object)
      → ∀(y : object)
      → ∀(fn : cat.arrow { _1 = x, _2 = y })
      → ∀(input : cat.arrow { _1 = c, _2 = x })
      → cat.arrow { _1 = c, _2 = y }
  }

precomposition (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(c : object)

        ∀(x : object)
      → ∀(y : object)
      → ∀(fn : cat.arrow { _1 = y, _2 = x })
      → ∀(input : cat.arrow { _1 = x, _2 = c })

    : { arrow :

      }
    )

    : { map :
            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : dObject)

      }

            ∀(a : dObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = g b }

      }
    )

{- NB: Since this is currently forced to be in *Set*, it’s quite possible that some of the uses of _C_ and _D_ are wrong, since the type system can’t distinguish them. So take them with a grain of salt if you’re editing this file. -}

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ ∀ ( vCategory
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : Type)
                  → v.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → v.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → v.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : Type) → v.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → cObject
      , unit :
          cObject
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : Type → Type)
→ ∀ ( fMonoidal
    : { map :
          ∀(a : Type) → ∀(b : Type) → v.arrow { _1 = a → b, _2 = f a → f b }
      , product :
            ∀(a : Type)
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(b : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
                  → ({ _1 : b._1, _2 : b._2 } → a)
                  → { _1 : f b._1, _2 : f b._2 }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → f a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : Type) → ({} → a) → f a
      }
    )
→ ∀(g : cObject → Type)
→ ∀ ( gMonoidal
    : { map :
            ∀(a : cObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → v.arrow { _1 = c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = g a → g b }
      , product :
            ∀(a : cObject)
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(b : { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject })
                  → c.arrow { _1 = c.product b, _2 = a }
                  → { _1 : g b._1, _2 : g b._2 }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → g a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = c.unit, _2 = a } → g a
      }
    )
→ { map :
        ∀(a : cObject)
      → ∀(b : cObject)
      → v.arrow { _1 = c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = f (g a) → f (g b) }
  , product :
        ∀(i : cObject)
      → ∀ ( day
          :   ∀(r : Type)
            → (   ∀(b : { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject })
                → c.arrow { _1 = c.product b, _2 = i }
                → { _1 : f (g b._1), _2 : f (g b._2) }
                → r
              )
            → r
          )
      → f (g i)
  , unit :
      ∀(a : cObject) → ∀(fn : c.arrow { _1 = c.unit, _2 = a }) → f (g a)
  }

Type (type)

{- A duoid (also known as a “united monoid”) is actually a pair of monoids with a shared `unit`. The `additive.product` distributes over the `multiplicative.product` as well. -}

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object)
→ { additive :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  , multiplicative :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

      m → m → Bool
  , multiply :
      { _1 : m, _2 : m } → m
  , negate :
      m → m
  , one :
      {} → m
  , partialLE :
      m → m → Optional Bool
  , reciprocal :
      m → m
  , subtract :
      ∀(x : { _1 : m, _2 : m }) → m
  , zero :
      {} → m
  }

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object)
→ { additive :
      { inverse :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
      , product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  , multiplicative :
      { inverse :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
      , product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }

divide (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → { _1 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit }, _2 = a }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ ∀ ( field
    : { additive :
          { inverse :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
          , product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      , multiplicative :
          { inverse :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
          , product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      }
    )
→ cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }

./Functor

./Functor/Bifunctor

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀(eObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → vObject
      , unit :
          vObject
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : eObject, _2 : eObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          eObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → eObject)
→ Type
type
  λ(vObject : Kind)
→ λ(cObject : Kind)
→ λ(dObject : Kind)
→ λ(eObject : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → vObject
      , unit :
          vObject
      }
    )
→ λ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : eObject, _2 : eObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          eObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ(f : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → eObject)
→ { map :
        ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
      → ∀(b : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            v.product
            { _1 =
                c.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 =
                d@1.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
        , _2 =
            d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
        }
  }

impliedFirstFunctor (term)

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( dCategory
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : dObject)
                  → d.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → d.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → d.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(eObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( e
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : eObject, _2 : eObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          eObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject } → eObject)
→ ∀ ( bifunctor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
          → { _1 :
                c.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                d.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → e.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
      }
    )
→ ∀(a : dObject)
→ { map :
        ∀(g : cObject)
      → ∀(h : cObject)
      → ∀(fn : c.arrow { _1 = g, _2 = h })
      → e.arrow { _1 = f { _1 = g, _2 = a }, _2 = f { _1 = h, _2 = a } }
  }

type
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cCategory
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : cObject)
                  → c.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → c.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → c.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : cObject) → c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(eObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( e
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : eObject, _2 : eObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          eObject → Type
      }
    )

→ ∀ ( bifunctor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : cObject, _2 : dObject })
          → { _1 :
                c.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                d.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → e.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
      }
    )
→ ∀(a : cObject)
→ { map :
        ∀(b : dObject)
      → ∀(c : dObject)
      → ∀(fn : d.arrow { _1 = b, _2 = c })
      → e.arrow { _1 = f { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = f { _1 = a, _2 = c } }
  }

Contravariant (type)

{- A contravariant functor `C → D` is equivalent to a covariant functor `C^op → D`. -}

kind
  ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(dObject : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : cObject → dObject)
→ Type
type
  λ(vObject : Kind)
→ λ(cObject : Kind)
→ λ(dObject : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → vObject
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ(f : cObject → dObject)
→ { map :
        ∀(a : cObject)
      → ∀(b : cObject)
      → v.arrow
        { _1 = c.arrow { _1 = b, _2 = a }, _2 = d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b } }
  }

Costar (type)

{- A functor from a Cokleisli category to the underlying category -}

kind
  ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → vObject
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object → object)
→ ∀(f : object → object)
→ Type
type
  λ(vObject : Kind)
→ λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → vObject
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object → object)
→ λ(f : object → object)
→ { map :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → v.arrow
        { _1 =
            cat.arrow { _1 = m b, _2 = a }
        , _2 =
            cat.arrow { _1 = f b, _2 = f a }
        }
  }

./Functor/Endo

./Functor/Endo/Star

Type (type)

{- This is very similar to Haskell’s `Traversable`, except that it can be implemented for an arbitrary `m`, doesn’t necessarily require an `Applicative` instance, and also may be _more_ constrained than `Applicative`. -}

kind
  ∀(vObject : Kind)
→ ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : vObject, _2 : vObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          vObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :

sequence (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : object → object)
→ ∀(g : object → object)
→ ∀ ( functor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = f b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = g a, _2 = f (g b) }
      }
    )
→ ∀(a : object)
→ cat.arrow { _1 = g (f a), _2 = f (g a) }

  ∀(object : Kind)

    : { arrow :

          Type → Type

      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )

    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )

./Functor/Monoidal

Type (type)

kind
  ∀(cObject : Kind)
→ ∀(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ ∀ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → cObject
      , unit :
          cObject
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : cObject → Type)
→ Type
type
  λ(cObject : Kind)
→ λ(v : { arrow : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type, constraint : Type → Type })
→ λ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → cObject
      , unit :
          cObject
      }
    )
→ λ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ(f : cObject → Type)
→ { map :
        ∀(a : cObject)
      → ∀(b : cObject)
      → v.arrow
        { _1 = c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b } }
  , product :
        ∀(a : cObject)
      → d.arrow
        { _1 =
              ∀(r : Type)
            → (   ∀(b : { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject })
                → c.arrow { _1 = c.product b, _2 = a }
                → d.product { _1 = f b._1, _2 = f b._2 }
                → r
              )
            → r
        , _2 =
            f a
        }
  , unit :
        ∀(a : cObject)
      → d.arrow { _1 = c.arrow { _1 = c.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = f a }
  }

          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( d
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : dObject, _2 : dObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          dObject → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : { _1 : dObject, _2 : cObject } → Type)
→ Type
type
  λ(cObject : Kind)
→ λ(dObject : Kind)

    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , constraint :

      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )
→ λ ( c
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : cObject, _2 : cObject } → Type
      , constraint :
          cObject → Type
      }
    )

functor (term)

{- If there is a natural transformation from `n` to `m`, then a m-Star functor can be made into an n-Star functor. -}

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : object → object)
→ { map :
        ∀(m : object → object)
      → ∀(n : object → object)
      → ∀(natural : ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = n a, _2 = m a })
      → ∀ ( star
          : { map :
                  ∀(a : object)
                → ∀(b : object)
                → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = m b }
                → cat.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
            }
          )
      → { map :
              ∀(a : object)
            → ∀(b : object)
            → ∀(fn : cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = n b })
            → cat.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
        }
  }

          ∀(a : Type) → ∀(b : Type) → (a → b) → d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
      }
    )
→ ∀(a : Type)
→ d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f {} }

Kind (kind)

{- A commutative monoid implies a preorder. However, that currently forces us into *Set*, so we instead just alias the non-commutative type to avoid specializing. -}

sort
  ∀(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ ∀(m : Kind)
→ Kind
kind
  λ(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ λ(m : Kind)
→ { inverse : cat.arrow m m, product : cat.arrow (cat.product m m) m, unit : m }

quotient (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → { _1 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit }, _2 = a }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ ∀ ( group
    : { inverse :
          cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
      , product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
    )
→ cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }

Type (type)

{- This is the weakest form of order provided. There is no standalone preorder, partial order, or anything, because there are too many possible instances. For the general case, just define regular functions. A `Group/PartiallyOrdered` constrains the instances enough for a generic “less than” to be meaningful. -}

      {} → m

./Groupoid

Type (type)

→ ∀ ( v
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type

      , product :

      }

    : { arrow :

      , constraint :
          Type → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : Type, _2 : Type } → Type
      , unit :
          Type
      }
    )

      }

              → r
            )
          → r

    )

      ∀(a : Type) → ∀(b : Type) → (a → b) → f a → f b
  , product :
        ∀(i : Type)
      → ∀ ( day
          :   ∀(r : Type)
            → (   ∀(b : { _1 : Type, _2 : Type })
                → ({ _1 : b._1, _2 : b._2 } → i)
                → { _1 : f b._1, _2 : f b._2 }
                → r
              )
            → r
          )
      → f i
  , unit :
      ∀(a : Type) → ∀(fn : {} → a) → f a
  }

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( semigroupoid
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object → object)
→ ∀ ( functor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = m a, _2 = m b }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( monad
    : { product :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = m (m a), _2 = m a }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = m a }
      }
    )

        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( semigroupoid
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object → object)
→ ∀ ( functor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = m a, _2 = m b }
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( monad
    : { product :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = m (m a), _2 = m a }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = m a }
      }
    )
→ { bind :

      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀(f : cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = m b })
      → cat.arrow { _1 = m a, _2 = m b }
  , extractStarfunctor :
      { map :

          → ∀(b : object)

      → ∀(b : object)

      ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = m a }

./Monoid/Commutative

Kind (kind)

{- A commutative monoid implies a preorder. However, that currently forces us into *Set*, so we instead just alias the non-commutative type to avoid specializing. -}

sort
  ∀(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ ∀(m : Kind)
→ Kind
kind
  λ(cat : { arrow : Kind → Kind → Kind, product : Kind → Kind → Kind })
→ λ(m : Kind)
→ { product : cat.arrow (cat.product m m) m, unit : m }

Set (type)

{- A commutative monoid implies a preorder. Technically, a preorder could be defined with `≤` where both `x ≤ y` and `y ≤ x` may be false. However, with structural typing it makes it impossible to distinguish a preordered structure from a totally-ordered structure. -}

kind
∀(m : Type) → Type
type
  λ(m : Type)
→ { preLE :
      m → m → Optional Bool
  , product :
      { _1 : m, _2 : m } → m
  , unit :
      {} → m
  }

  }

      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

      , product :

subtract (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( category
    : { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → { _1 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit }, _2 = a }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ ∀ ( ring
    : { additive :
          { inverse :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
          , product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      , multiplicative :
          { product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      }
    )
→ cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )

    : { associativity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → ∀(b : object)
          → ∀(c : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                }
            , to :
                cat.arrow
                { _1 =
                    cat.product { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = b }, _2 = c }
                , _2 =
                    cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = c } }
                }
            }
      , leftIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
            }
      , map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → { _1 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
      , product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      , rightIdentity :
            ∀(a : object)
          → { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit } }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = cat.unit }, _2 = a }
            }
      , unit :
          ∀(a : object) → cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)

    : { additive :
          { inverse :
              cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }
          , product :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }

              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }

              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
          , unit :
              cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
          }
      }
    )

      cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }

      cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }

      cat.arrow { _1 = m, _2 = m }

functor (term)

type
  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( semigroupoid
    : { product :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → (   ∀(r : Type)
              → (   ∀(z : object)
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = z, _2 = a._2 }
                  → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = z }
                  → r
                )
              → r
            )
          → cat.arrow a
      }
    )
→ ∀ ( bifunctor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → ∀(b : { _1 : object, _2 : object })
          → { _1 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = b._1 }
            , _2 :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a._2, _2 = b._2 }
            }
          → cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product a, _2 = cat.product b }
      }
    )
→ { map :
        ∀(a : object)
      → ∀(b : object)
      → ∀ ( fn
          : { from :
                cat.arrow { _1 = b, _2 = a }
            , to :
                cat.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
            }
          )
      → ∀ ( fa
          : { product :
                cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = a, _2 = a }, _2 = a }
            }
          )
      → { product : cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = b, _2 = b }, _2 = b } }
  }

{- This is different from what is often called a “semiring” as it lacks additive unit, but here we follow the convention described in https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/rig, using the name “rig” for what would traditionally be a semiring. -}

  ∀(object : Kind)
→ ∀ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :

      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ ∀(m : object)
→ Type
type
  λ(object : Kind)
→ λ ( cat
    : { arrow :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → Type
      , constraint :
          object → Type
      , product :
          { _1 : object, _2 : object } → object
      , unit :
          object
      }
    )
→ λ(m : object)
→ { additive :
      { product : cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m } }
  , multiplicative :
      { product :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.product { _1 = m, _2 = m }, _2 = m }
      , unit :
          cat.arrow { _1 = cat.unit, _2 = m }
      }
  }

      }

                )
              → r

          → cat.arrow a
      }
    )

    : { map :

      }
    )

                → r
              )
            → r
          )
      → cat.arrow { _1 = a._1, _2 = m a._2 }

          ∀(a : dObject) → d.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = a }
      }
    )
→ ∀(f : cObject → dObject)
→ ∀ ( functor
    : { map :
            ∀(a : cObject)
          → ∀(b : cObject)
          → c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b }
          → d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
      }
    )
→ ∀(a : cObject)
→ ∀(b : cObject)
→ ∀(k : c.arrow { _1 = a, _2 = b })
→ d.arrow { _1 = f a, _2 = f b }
